# Changelog

## 2026-06-23 (feat: /speak works in full group chats, not just Lite NPCs)
- **Files changed**:
  - lib/services/chat/chat_command_handler.dart — `/speak` now routes to a group branch when getGroupMembers() is non-empty (mirrors how /exit already routes), forcing the named member to take their turn now. Member name-resolution (exact -> unique substring -> empty/ambiguous/unknown errors) is consolidated into a new shared `_resolveGroupMember` used by BOTH /speak and /exit — the old inline /exit resolution is deleted (no duplicate logic). /speak command-registry description updated.
  - lib/services/chat_service.dart — wired the `speakGroupMember` callback: `setNextSpeaker(member)` + `_generateResponse(GenerationMode.normal)`, the same path the goodbye narration uses, minus the removal/directive.
  - test/services/chat/chat_command_handler_test.dart — +5 /speak group tests (forces by name, unique substring, empty asks who, unknown + ambiguous speak nobody). 52 handler tests pass.
  - docs/Rawhide.md — user-facing bullets for /speak-in-groups, the bidirectional RAG carry, and the Group Card origin reconnect.
- **Reason**: /speak (force a present character to take their turn now) only worked for Lite NPC scene guests; in a full group it did nothing useful. Now it forces a full member by name, completing /join + /exit + /speak group-macro parity with the lite scene.
- **Verification**: flutter analyze clean; 52 command-handler tests pass; full chat suite green. Reviewed (speak-parity dimension): /exit behavior unchanged by the consolidation, single realism/needs eval, post-gen checks intact. Known no-op nit (consistent with ALL direct-generate paths — goodbye narration, director notes, auto-play — NOT a regression): a /speak-forced bubble shows no per-message needs-delta CHIP (the simulation runs correctly; only the chip widget lives in sendMessage). Out of scope to refactor here.
- **Commit hash**: (uncommitted)


## 2026-06-23 (feat: RAG memory now carries 1:1 -> group on /join — recall of pre-conversion events)
- **Files changed**:
  - lib/database/database.dart — new `copyEmbeddingsForSession(fromCharacterId, fromSessionId, {toCharacterId, toSessionId})`: COPIES a character's RAG embeddings for one session under a new character id + session id (fresh row ids via insertEmbeddings), leaving the originals untouched. COPY — not the collapse direction's in-place `reassignEmbeddings` re-key — because the source 1:1 is preserved as the revert snapshot and must keep its own memory. No schema/build_runner change (query method, not a table change).
  - lib/services/chat/chat_service_cast.dart — `_carryHostStateIntoForkedGroup` now also copies the host's 1:1 semantic memory into the GROUP's shared pool: from (originalCharId, hostSessionId) to (`_getCharacterId()` = 'group_<id>', the new group session). Folded into the existing objectives-copy guard (no new guard); comments trimmed to keep the file at 499 lines (<500 cap).
- **Reason**: converting a 1:1 to a group with /join copied the messages + summary but NOT the RAG embedding index, which is keyed by character id ('group_<id>' for groups, library id for 1:1). So the group character could not semantically recall pre-conversion events that had scrolled out of the context window. Now it can. (The reverse — group->1:1 collapse — already carried memory via `reassignEmbeddings`; independently verified lossless in the same review.)
- **Verification**: flutter analyze clean; chat_service_cast.dart 499 lines; full chat/model test suites pass. Adversarially reviewed (rag-fork + rag-collapse dimensions): COPY semantics, source/target keys, and collapse losslessness all confirmed; zero defects.
- **Commit hash**: (uncommitted)


## 2026-06-23 (feat: Group Cards carry each member's true library origin so re-imports reconnect — Phase 4)
- **Files changed**:
  - lib/ui/pages/home_page.dart — group-card EXPORT now writes a per-member `_origin_library_stable_id` = `m.originStableId` (the source library character's stableGroupId) into raw_member_data, DISTINCT from the existing `_original_stable_id` (the export INSTANCE id used only for realism relationship remap). IMPORT now stamps `group_members.memberState` via `GroupMember.encodeProvenance(originStableId: ...)` instead of the old hardcoded `const Value('{}')`, so a re-imported member is reconnectable by MemberOriginResolver (exact stableGroupId on the same machine, name fallback cross-machine). The read is tolerant (`is String`, not a hard cast) so a malformed/foreign non-string value degrades to origin-unknown '{}' rather than dropping the whole member. The machine-local `originLibraryDbId` is deliberately NOT exported (zero read sites; meaningless on another device).
  - lib/models/group_member.dart — corrected the now-stale `originStableId` getter + `encodeProvenance` docstrings (import DOES stamp now, from the portable key — not '{}' forever).
  - test/models/character_card_test.dart — new round-trip test: both keys survive export/import independently; an origin-unknown member stays keyless (no false origin); the encodeProvenance stamping contract yields the right blob / '{}'.
  - docs/characters.md, docs/CharacterCardForge_GroupChat_Integration_Guide.md — documented the new optional additive (spec_version 1.0, NO bump) per-member key for external tools (Character Card Forge); noted it is separate from `_original_stable_id` and that `originLibraryDbId` must never be emitted.
- **Reason**: Phase 4 of "one chat, changing cast". Imported group members were origin-unknown ('{}'), so a re-imported group couldn't reconnect members to the local library (collapsing it back to a 1:1 had to guess by name only). Now the portable card carries the real origin.
- **Verification**: flutter analyze clean (full project); flutter test test/models/ test/services/chat/ all pass (incl. new round-trip). group_card.dart unchanged (rawMemberData passes the key opaquely); group_member.dart doc-only. Adversarially reviewed (5-dim workflow): zero confirmed defects; the lone low finding (hard-cast import drop) fixed here.
- **Commit hash**: (uncommitted)


## 2026-06-23 (feat: /exit a full group member now narrates a goodbye + offers a lossless deferred-deletion UNDO)
- **Files changed**:
  - lib/services/chat/chat_service_cast.dart — reworked `exitGroupMember` from "narrate then immediately delete" into a deferred-deletion flow: (1) the leaving member narrates their own goodbye via the one-shot `_entranceDirective`; (2) they are SOFT-removed from the live roster only (`_groupManager.refreshCharacters(remaining)`) — their DB row / realism / evolution / quests / memory are left fully intact; (3) `_pendingMemberExit` is set and the UNDO snackbar is armed (`_exitUndoMessage` = goodbye turn, `_exitUndoOfferName` = member name, deliberately WITHOUT the lite `_exitUndoGuest` marker). Added `_commitPendingMemberExit()` which runs the real removal (`removeCharacterFromGroup`, incl. any auto-collapse to 1:1) when the undo window closes. `exitGroupMember` also commits any prior pending exit first (UNDO only applies to the most recent `/exit`) and re-checks `_activeGroup` / membership afterward, so back-to-back `/exit` can't orphan a soft-removed member.
  - lib/services/chat/chat_service_group_membership.dart — extracted the member re-resolve loop into a shared `_reloadGroupRoster()` (reads `_groupChatRepository`, resolves avatars, pushes to the turn manager, returns the cards). `removeCharacterFromGroup` now calls it; the undo reuses it to bring the soft-removed member straight back.
  - lib/services/chat_service.dart — added `_pendingMemberExit` field; `undoLastExit` gained a group branch (delete the goodbye turn via `deleteMessage` so its realism rolls back, then `_reloadGroupRoster` to restore the member); `_clearExitUndo` now also nulls `_pendingMemberExit` (so a context switch / new chat safely CANCELS a pending exit — the row was never deleted); `sendMessage`'s "undo window ends" point now calls `await _commitPendingMemberExit()` before `_clearExitUndo()` so continuing the conversation finalizes the removal in the settled cast. The `removeGroupMember` callback comment updated.
- **Reason**: in a full group, `/exit` deleted the member instantly with no goodbye and no undo — unlike the Lite-NPC `/exit`, which narrates a departure and offers UNDO. A full member is a real DB row (deleting one can also auto-collapse the group to a 1:1), so a true lossless undo required deferring the destructive delete until the user continues rather than snapshotting/recreating state.
- **Verification**: `flutter analyze` clean (chat_service + chat/ leaves + chat_page); `flutter test test/services/chat/` → all 365 pass (incl. command-handler 47, realism parity). cast.dart 485 lines / group_membership.dart 496 lines (both under the 500 cap). pubspec.lock dep bumps (matcher/test_api) left uncommitted — unrelated churn.
- **Commit hash**: (uncommitted)


## 2026-06-23 (fix: /join --full opens the character picker too — no more needing an exact name)
- **Files changed**:
  - lib/services/chat/chat_command_handler.dart — the `requestGuestPicker` callback now takes a `full` flag. `/join --full` with no name, or with an ambiguous/no match, now OPENS the picker (pre-filtered to any typed text) instead of erroring with "name a character" / "use the full name". Lite `/join` is unchanged (passes `full: false`).
  - lib/services/chat_service.dart — added `_pendingGuestPickerFull` + `pendingGuestPickerFull` getter; reset on dismiss; wired into the picker-request callback.
  - lib/ui/pages/chat_page.dart — `_showGuestPickerDialog` now reads the full flag: in full mode it lists `joinableGroupCharacters` (in a group) or `joinableGuestCharacters` (1:1 convert) and, on pick, calls `joinFull`; in lite mode it lists guests and calls `joinSceneGuest`.
  - test/services/chat/chat_command_handler_test.dart — updated the picker stub to the 2-arg signature; the two "full needs an exact name" tests now assert the picker opens (full flag true).
- **Reason**: `/join --full` (and `/join` in a group, which is always full) previously required typing the character's exact name — the picker only worked for lite `/join`. Now the full path gets the same browsable picker.
- **Verification**: `flutter analyze` clean; `flutter test test/services/chat/ test/models/` → all 532 pass.
- **Commit hash**: (uncommitted)


## 2026-06-23 (fix: persist NSFW cooldown TOTAL so arousal refractory survives reload — sessions schema add)
- **Files changed**:
  - lib/database/database.dart — added `cooldownTurnsTotal` IntColumn (default 0) to the Sessions table, and `'cooldown_turns_total INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0'` to the `_repairMissingSchemaColumns` `columnsToEnsure['sessions']` list so existing user DBs ALTER it in on next launch (with the automatic timestamped backup the repair already takes). schemaVersion unchanged (32) — this matches how the other realism columns were added (the always-on repair, not onUpgrade).
  - lib/database/database.g.dart — regenerated (`dart run build_runner build`); the generated column is `cooldown_turns_total`, matching the repair entry exactly.
  - lib/services/chat/chat_service_session_state.dart — `_doSaveChat` now writes `cooldownTurnsTotal: _nsfwService.cooldownTurnsTotal`.
  - lib/services/chat/chat_service_session_load.dart — both load paths (`_loadLastSession`, `loadSession`) now pass `cooldownTurnsTotal: session.cooldownTurnsTotal` to `loadNsfwScalars` (which already accepted the param).
- **Reason**: The NSFW arousal refractory tracks BOTH "cooldown turns remaining" and the TOTAL it started from (the denominator for the cooldown progress). Only "remaining" had a session column, so on a normal 1:1 reload the total reset to 0 — losing the refractory context (a real part of the Realism Engine, per the maintainer). It already carried across 1:1<->group conversion via the realism snapshot; this fixes the plain reload. Maintainer explicitly approved the sessions schema change.
- **Forge compatibility**: the new column is `INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0`, so Character Card Forge's direct `sessions` INSERTs that omit it use the default and keep working — backward compatible.
- **Verification**: `flutter analyze` clean; FULL `flutter test` suite passes (1369 tests). Generated SQL column name (`cooldown_turns_total`) confirmed to match the repair-list entry. Only the 4 intended source files + the regenerated `.g.dart` changed.
- **Commit hash**: (uncommitted)


## 2026-06-23 (feat: make 1:1<->group conversion lossless — carry flags/evolution/objectives/author-notes/RAG both directions)
- **Files changed**:
  - lib/database/database.dart — new `reassignObjectives(from,to,{chatId})` and `reassignEmbeddings(from,to,{chatId})` (UPDATE-by-characterId re-key methods; both bump sync version). No schema change.
  - lib/services/chat/chat_service_group_membership.dart — `forkToGroupChat` now captures a FULL host-state bundle (realism snapshot — realism-gated — plus the enable-flags, author note, and evolution — captured unconditionally) and the host's 1:1 session id, passed to the carry. Helper moved out to the cast leaf to stay under 500 lines.
  - lib/services/chat/chat_service_cast.dart — `_carryHostStateIntoForkedGroup` (fork) and `_collapseGroupToSolo` (collapse) now carry, BOTH directions: realism values, the enable-flags (realismEnabled/needsSimEnabled/**nsfwCooldownEnabled**/passageOfTimeEnabled/chaosModeEnabled+pressure), per-character author notes, character evolution (personality/scenario into the group_evolved_* JSON columns on fork / the 1:1 evolved* columns on collapse), objectives (COPIED onto the member on fork incl. injectionDepth; **RE-KEYED instead of deleted** on collapse), and group-era RAG embeddings (**re-keyed** group_<id> -> origin library id on collapse instead of wiped). Flags/author/evolution/objectives carry regardless of realism; only realism values are realism-gated.
- **Reason**: An audit (5-agent sweep) found the conversion carry was missing a whole class of per-character/session state — only realism values carried, so evolution, quests, the NSFW-enhancement toggle, author notes, RAG memory, and other flags reset on convert/collapse. Realism values + chat summary + session name already round-tripped; everything else now does too.
- **Verification**: `flutter analyze` clean; 540 tests pass. A 3-dimension adversarial review confirmed keys/DB-methods/re-key-targets/round-trip correct and caught: **(HIGH)** the fork carry being realism-gated (dropping flags/author/evolution/objectives for realism-off chats) → fixed (now unconditional, symmetric with collapse); **(MEDIUM)** the objectives copy dropping `injectionDepth` → fixed; **(LOW)** a stale per-char NSFW flag read on collapse → fixed (read from the group store). No collision risk (member ids are fresh UUIDs distinct from library ids).
- **Known limitations (documented, NOT regressions — "lossless" caveats)**: group evolution COUNT is mem-only (pre-existing — survives within a session but a group reload resets it to 0; the evolved TEXT round-trips fine). Deferred (need maintainer OK — they touch the Forge-written `sessions` schema): per-character system-prompt override carry, and a `cooldownTurnsTotal` column. Also deferred (heavier, unreported): copying the 1:1's PRIOR RAG memory INTO a new group on fork (the group→1:1 direction is done); data-bank rows are dropped on collapse (rarely used).
- **Commit hash**: (uncommitted)


## 2026-06-23 (feat: /join and /exit macros now work in full group chats, not just 1:1)
- **Files changed**:
  - lib/services/chat/chat_command_handler.dart — `/exit <name>` now removes a FULL group member (new `_handleGroupMemberExit`, branches at the top of `_handleExit` when a group roster is present — Scene Guests are 1:1-only so a non-empty roster means a full group; guards against removing the only remaining member). `/join` is now group-aware: it works in a group (the old hard `_activeCharacterIsSet()` 1:1-only guard is replaced with "open a chat first"), and inside a group a plain `/join <name>` (or `--lite`) silently becomes a full join (groups have no lite tier). Added 3 callbacks (getGroupMembers / getGroupJoinableCharacters / removeGroupMember). Help text for both commands updated.
  - lib/services/chat_service.dart — wired the 3 new command callbacks; new `joinableGroupCharacters` getter (library minus current members by name; addCharacterToGroup's D5 stable-identity guard is the real backstop).
  - lib/ui/pages/chat_page.dart — removed the sidebar "Add Character" button (adding a member is now `/join <name>`, surfaced by the "type /" command helper) and deleted the now-dead `_showAddCharacterToGroupDialog` + its unused `path` import — frees sidebar space / cleaner UI.
  - test/services/chat/chat_command_handler_test.dart — updated the "no chat open" rejection test and added 6 group cases (/join routes to full, /join --full adds, /exit removes a member, /exit no-name asks, /exit unknown name, /exit can't remove the last).
- **Reason**: Macros should work the same in groups and 1:1 — users hit "only works in 1:1 chats" on `/join --full` and found `/exit` couldn't remove full members (only Lite NPCs). The underlying `joinFull` (→ addCharacterToGroup, Phase 2) and `removeCharacterFromGroup` (→ real removal + auto-collapse, Phase 3) already handle groups; this just wires the macros to them and removes the now-redundant sidebar button.
- **Verification**: `flutter analyze` clean; `flutter test test/services/chat/ test/services/group_entrance_test.dart test/models/` → all 540 pass (incl. the 6 new group-command tests). One new private method (`_handleGroupMemberExit`). The "…" menu's separate "Add Character (Group)…" (fork_group) entry was left as-is (possible follow-up cleanup). No commit yet (uncommitted on branch claude/unify-chat-interfaces-tyzeb4).
- **Commit hash**: (uncommitted)


## 2026-06-23 (feat: Phase 3 of "one chat, changing cast" — real member removal + auto-collapse group→1:1)
- **Files changed**:
  - lib/database/database.dart — new `deleteGroupMember(memberId)` (single-row delete; complements the existing per-group delete).
  - lib/services/chat/chat_service_cast.dart (NEW leaf, part of chat_service) — `_deleteMemberCleanup(charId, avatarFilename)`: deletes the member's DB row + private avatar + per-member persisted state (objectives/embeddings/data-bank, all keyed by the member's unique instance id so scoped deletes are safe) + the EIGHT in-memory maps (the six realism/notes/prompts/RAG/objectives + the three evolution maps the old stub never touched). `_collapseGroupToSolo(groupRepo)`: when a removal leaves one member, resolves its origin library character via Phase 1 `MemberOriginResolver`, then carries the survivor's realism BACK into 1:1 scalars (inverse of Phase 2 — load into scalars in group mode, snapshot, re-home the session, restore after, `_saveChat`), re-homes the CURRENT session in place (patchSession groupId→null, characterId→origin.dbId, createdAt bumped so re-entry lands on it), dissolves the now-empty group (member rows + private avatars + definition), and re-enters as a 1:1 keeping all history.
  - lib/services/chat/chat_service_group_membership.dart — `removeCharacterFromGroup` rewritten from a broken stub (it refreshed the roster with an EMPTY list and deleted nothing) to a real delete + survivor re-resolve + `_saveChat` + auto-collapse trigger.
  - lib/services/chat_service.dart — registered the cast part + imported MemberOriginResolver.
  - lib/ui/pages/chat_page.dart, lib/services/web_server_service.dart, assets/web/js/app.js — remove gate relaxed `>2`→`>1` (allow removing the second-to-last → collapse); web remove handler now resolves the target against the LIVE group members (instance id) instead of the library (which silently matched nothing); stale "min 2 required" copy fixed.
- **Reason**: Phase 3 of the "one chat, a cast that changes" unification — the completion of the user's original ask ("collapse a group back to a 1:1 with the original character, no dupes floating around"). A one-character group is nonsense, so collapse is automatic (user decision) the instant a removal leaves one member; if the survivor's origin can't be resolved it stays a one-member cast rather than guessing.
- **Verification**: `flutter analyze` clean; 534 tests pass. Adversarially verified by a 3-dimension review (reverse-carry-parity / session-rehome-orphans / removal-trigger-regressions) which confirmed the reverse carry + re-home ordering are sound and caught: **(HIGH)** collapse dissolving OTHER group sessions' history → guarded (only auto-dissolve when this is the group's only session; otherwise surface a banner and stay a cast); **(HIGH)** survivor objectives/embeddings/data-bank orphaned → cleaned up on collapse (group-era quests + semantic memory don't carry to the 1:1 — messages + realism do; re-keying for full continuity is a future refinement); **(HIGH)** the web remove endpoint matching the wrong id space → fixed; **(MEDIUM)** evolution maps not cleaned on removal → added; **(LOW)** unchecked patchSession + non-atomic re-home/dissolve → patchSession result now checked and aborts before dissolving; **(LOW)** silent dead-end on failed collapse → now surfaces a banner. Definitive check is the user: convert 1:1→group, remove the others, confirm landing in a clean 1:1 with the original character (history + realism intact). No commit yet (uncommitted on branch claude/unify-chat-interfaces-tyzeb4).
- **Commit hash**: (uncommitted)


## 2026-06-23 (feat: Phase 2 of "one chat, changing cast" — carry host realism across 1:1→group + D5 guard)
- **Files changed**:
  - lib/services/chat/chat_service_group_membership.dart — `forkToGroupChat` now (1) captures the host's live 1:1 realism (`_captureRealismState()`) at the TOP while still 1:1, and (2) after `setActiveGroup` switches into group mode, calls the new `_carryHostRealismIntoForkedGroup(...)` which restores that snapshot onto the host MEMBER's per-character store (keyed by the member instance id) via the same path regenerate uses (`restoreFromMessageState` + `restoreNsfwFromMessageState` + `restoreTimeFromRealismState` + needs vector) and the canonical `_saveScalarsIntoGroupRealism` write, then `_saveChat`. Fixes the realism-reset-on-convert (/promote) bug. Also: (a) D5 dedup of arrivals inside `forkToGroupChat` (drops any arrival repeating the host or another arrival by stable identity — the single chokepoint for in-app AND web `/api/groups/fork`), and (b) a D5 guard in `addCharacterToGroup` rejecting a live add of a character already present (matched by Phase 0 `originStableId`, name fallback for legacy), with an "already in this chat" banner. One new private method (`_carryHostRealismIntoForkedGroup`).
  - lib/services/chat_service.dart — `joinFull` no longer clobbers the specific D5 banner with a generic "could not add" message on a failed add.
- **Reason**: Phase 2 of the "one chat, a cast that changes" unification. Per the user's decisions: keep the proven fork (the original 1:1 session it leaves untouched IS the D3 revert snapshot — no new copy needed) and add ONLY the realism carry + the D5 one-instance-per-character guard. Converting a 1:1 to a group previously reset the host's bond/trust/emotion/arousal/fixation/needs/time because the host's scalar realism was never written into the new group session's `group_realism_state` under the host member's key — so the group loaded realism OFF. The carry closes that gap while preserving 1:1↔group parity (same observable realism before/after convert).
- **Verification**: `flutter analyze` clean; `flutter test test/services/chat/ test/services/group_entrance_test.dart test/models/` → all 534 pass (incl. the realism parity gate). Adversarially verified by a 3-dimension review (carry-key-correctness / ordering-parity / D5-regressions): it confirmed the carry key matches end-to-end (host realism written and read under the same member instance id) and caught **(HIGH)** the carry dropping narrative time → fixed by adding `_timeService.restoreTimeFromRealismState`, **(MEDIUM)** the web/conversion path bypassing D5 → fixed by the arrivals dedup, and **(LOW)** the joinFull banner clobber + a needs-enabled-but-empty-vector edge → both fixed. Known-accepted (not regressions): the 3 long-term accumulators (turnsSinceLongTermCheck/shortTermDeltasSummary/moodDecayCounter) aren't per-character-persisted — a pre-existing `_groupRealism` schema limitation affecting all members equally, tracked for a future store-schema parity pass. Definitive check is the user running `/promote` and watching realism persist. No commit yet (uncommitted on branch claude/unify-chat-interfaces-tyzeb4).
- **Commit hash**: (uncommitted)


## 2026-06-23 (feat: Phase 1 of "one chat, changing cast" — best-effort member→library origin resolver)
- **Files changed**:
  - lib/services/chat/member_origin_resolver.dart (NEW, ~85 lines) — Pure, dependency-free `MemberOriginResolver.resolve({stampedOriginStableId, memberName, libraryCharacters})` returning the origin library `CharacterCard?` for a group member. Precedence: (1) authoritative — a stamped `originStableId` (Phase 0) that still exists in the library, matched by `stableGroupId`; (2) best-effort fallback — when there is no usable stamp (legacy `{}` member, OR a stamped origin whose target has been deleted/re-imported), a UNIQUE case-insensitive, whitespace-trimmed match on the member's name. Conservative by design: zero or ambiguous (2+) name matches, or an empty name, return `null` ("origin unknown — stay a cast", never an error). Pure so the rules are unit-testable in isolation.
  - test/services/chat/member_origin_resolver_test.dart (NEW, 11 tests) — Covers stamp-hit, stamp-wins-over-name, legacy unique-name match, ambiguous-name → null, no-match → null, blank-stamp → name fallback, stamped-but-missing → name fallback, stamped-missing + ambiguous → null, empty-name → null, case/whitespace insensitivity, and empty-library → null.
- **Reason**: Phase 1 of the "one chat, a cast that changes" unification. Members created BEFORE Phase 0's provenance stamping have no origin link (their `memberState` was `{}`), and group-card imports are intentionally origin-unknown. This resolver lets later phases reconnect such legacy/imported members to their library character (best-effort by name) so a chat can collapse back to a 1:1 with the original. It is a pure building block: read-only, zero behavior change, no production consumer yet — the ChatService seam that feeds it the live library is added in the phase that collapses a chat (Phase 3), alongside its consumer, to avoid uncalled production code. The unit tests are its current exercise.
- **Verification**: `flutter analyze --no-fatal-warnings --no-fatal-infos` → "No issues found!". `flutter test test/services/chat/member_origin_resolver_test.dart` → 11/11 pass. No behavior change anywhere (the resolver is not yet wired into any flow). No commit yet (uncommitted on branch claude/unify-chat-interfaces-tyzeb4).
- **Commit hash**: (uncommitted)


## 2026-06-23 (feat: Phase 0 of "one chat, changing cast" — group-member provenance stamping)
- **Files changed**:
  - lib/models/group_member.dart — Added `originStableId` / `originLibraryDbId` getters (read the `memberState` blob, null-safe for legacy `{}` / non-string / empty) and a static `encodeProvenance({originStableId, originLibraryDbId})` that builds the `group_members.memberState` JSON (trims, omits blank/null, yields `{}` when nothing). Single source of truth for the blob shape so every creation site stamps identically. Doc lists the real creation sites and the deliberate import exception.
  - lib/services/chat/chat_service_group_membership.dart — `_createGroupMember` now stamps `memberState` via `GroupMember.encodeProvenance(originStableId: character.stableGroupId, originLibraryDbId: character.dbId)` instead of `'{}'`. This one method backs the 1:1→group fork (host + arrivals), live `/join` adds (addCharacterToGroup), and the web-API fork (via forkToGroupChat).
  - lib/ui/pages/create_group_chat_page.dart — the create-group wizard stamps from `source.stableGroupId` / `source.dbId`.
  - lib/services/web_server_service.dart — **Removed the redundant post-fork member-materialization loop** in the POST /api/groups/fork handler. `forkToGroupChat` already creates every member (host + each additional char) via `_createGroupMember`; the loop re-inserted each additional char a SECOND time under a fresh UUID with `memberState:'{}'` — a pre-existing double-insert bug that left duplicate, un-stamped rows (and duplicate avatar copies) on every web-API fork. Deleting it fixes the duplication and closes the provenance gap in one move (verified: forkToGroupChat creates a row for every arrival incl. silent ones; the add-character handler has no analogous pattern).
  - lib/ui/pages/home_page.dart — group-card IMPORT deliberately does NOT stamp provenance (documented inline). A Group Card export carries the exporter's per-member UUID (avatar basename) in `_original_stable_id`, not the source library `stableGroupId`, so there is no resolvable library origin to stamp; imported members stay origin-unknown (`{}`) and are reconnected by name in Phase 1. (Making the portable format carry true origin is Phase 4.)
  - test/models/group_member_provenance_test.dart (NEW) — round-trip of encode + getters, trim/omit-blank, legacy `{}` back-compat, and non-string/empty tolerance.
- **Reason**: Phase 0 of the "one chat, a cast that changes" unification (group/1:1 merge). A group member is a copy of a library character under a fresh UUID, so on its own it can't be traced back to the character it came from. Stamping the origin into the Forge-invisible `memberState` blob (no DB migration) is the foundation that lets later phases collapse a chat back to a 1:1 with the ORIGINAL character without orphaned duplicates. Phase 0 is a pure foundation: zero behavior change, full back-compat for legacy `{}` members.
- **Verification**: `flutter analyze --no-fatal-warnings --no-fatal-infos` → "No issues found!". `flutter test test/models/ test/services/chat/ test/services/group_entrance_test.dart` → all 523 pass. Adversarially verified by a 4-dimension review (missed-sites / stamp-correctness / back-compat-readers / forge-sync-export) which caught the missed web site + the pre-existing double-insert + a wrong import stamp — all fixed — plus a focused review confirming the web-handler loop deletion is regression-free. memberState is not written by Character Card Forge and not row-merged by cloud sync, so the stamp is Forge- and sync-safe. No commit yet (uncommitted on branch claude/unify-chat-interfaces-tyzeb4).
- **Commit hash**: (uncommitted)


## 2026-06-23 (feat: regenerate the main character even after a Lite NPC has replied)
- **Files changed**:
  - lib/services/chat_service.dart — Extracted the inline post-host-turn Scene Guest chime-in block from `sendMessage` into a private `_maybeRunSceneGuestChimeIns({required String userText})` (same guards/token/`runChimeIns` call, zero behaviour change for the send path) so the regen path can reuse the IDENTICAL chime-decision gate. Added a public getter `regenerableHostBelowGuestsIndex` → the index of the most recent host message that is buried only under one or more guest (Lite NPC) replies (null when the host is already last, when a user/System message breaks the guest tail, or outside 1:1).
  - lib/services/chat/chat_service_reprocess.dart — Added `regenerateMainCharacter()`: walks back past trailing guest replies to the host message, reconstructs the prompting user text, removes the now-stale guest replies from `_messages` (UI + context) + saves, then delegates to the existing `regenerateLastMessage()` for the host regen (so realism reverts to the previous accepted snapshot exactly as a normal regen — no parallel realism logic), then re-runs `_maybeRunSceneGuestChimeIns` so the NPC speaks again only if still relevant to the NEW reply. Delegates straight to `regenerateLastMessage()` when the host is already last.
  - lib/ui/chat_components/bubbles/message_bubble.dart — The action-button row now also renders a regen icon on a host bubble that is buried under guest replies (`index == regenerableHostBelowGuestsIndex`), wired to `regenerateMainCharacter()`, tooltip "Regenerate main character (removes the NPC’s reply)". Uses `AppColors.resolve(context, Colors.orangeAccent, Colors.orange.shade800)` (light-safe) to match the existing orange regen icon. The existing last-message regen (which can target the guest's own reply) is unchanged.
- **Reason**: In a 1:1 "lite group" (Scene Guests / Lite NPCs) the turn flow is user → main character → NPC chime-in. The regen button is hard-gated to the LAST bot message, so once the NPC replied the user could no longer regenerate the main character's response — only the NPC's. Per the requested behaviour: always remove the NPC's reply from UI + context, regenerate the main character, then re-check whether the NPC should respond to the new content (mention / relevance) rather than blindly re-chiming. Reuses `runChimeIns` (the existing chime gate) and `regenerateLastMessage` (existing realism-correct regen) — no parallel paths.
- **Verification**: `flutter analyze --no-fatal-warnings --no-fatal-infos` → "No issues found!". `flutter test test/services/chat/` → all 348 pass. Grepped new surface: `_maybeRunSceneGuestChimeIns` called from both `sendMessage` and the regen path (only `runChimeIns` site left), `regenerateMainCharacter` + `regenerableHostBelowGuestsIndex` referenced from `message_bubble.dart`; no orphaned inline block, no dead code. New private methods: 1 (`_maybeRunSceneGuestChimeIns`, an extraction that removes duplication). Group chats unaffected (all new logic guarded on 1:1 + guests present). No commit (uncommitted on branch claude/unify-chat-interfaces-tyzeb4).
- **Commit hash**: (uncommitted)


## 2026-06-23 (fix: loading a 1:1 chat nuked the character's saved realism state)
- **Files changed**:
  - lib/services/chat/chat_service_realism_dance.dart — In `_evaluateRealismForUpcomingSpeaker`, gated the `_groupRealism` load/save plumbing on `_activeGroup != null`. Previously the 1:1 host (`_activeGroup == null`) fell into the `else` branch and called `_loadGroupRealismIntoScalars(charId)`, then `_saveScalarsIntoGroupRealism(charId)` at the end. The group map's setters route through `_setGroupRealismValue`, which early-returns when `_activeGroup == null` (group-only store), while its getters (`getGroupAffectionScore` etc.) read the map with a 0/default fallback and are NOT gated. So for a 1:1 host the load read an empty map → reset bond→0, trust→default, fixation/emotion→empty, needs→fresh 100s, overwriting the state `loadSession` had just restored. Now the host operates directly on its scalar fields (the canonical 1:1 store), which already hold the loaded + post-decay values; the shared eval mutates them in place and `_saveChat` persists them as before. Group path unchanged.
  - lib/services/chat_service.dart — In `sendMessage`, removed the misleading 1:1-host "mirror post-decay realism into the cast store" block (`_saveScalarsIntoGroupRealism(_getCharacterId())` + its debugPrint). That mirror was a guaranteed no-op (the setter early-returns in 1:1) and only existed to feed the now-removed host reload. Kept the unified eval invocation (`_evaluateRealismForUpcomingSpeaker(_activeCharacter!)`).
- **Reason**: Regression introduced by the realism unification (commit ccae8b1 "collapse 1:1 + group onto ONE eval path"). The unified eval routed the 1:1 host through the group-only `_groupRealism` storage dance, but only the *read* side of that store has a 1:1 fallback; the *write* side is gated off in 1:1. The asymmetry meant the first post-load turn (and the realism UI) saw an empty store and wiped persisted bond/trust/emotion/fixation/needs. The eval *logic* unification (4-call + verifier + trust-repair shared by host and group) is preserved — only the per-character map plumbing is now correctly group-scoped, matching the documented "orchestration may differ (scalars vs map), observable behavior must not" parity rule.
- **Verification**: `flutter analyze --no-fatal-warnings --no-fatal-infos` → "No issues found!". `flutter test test/services/chat/` → all 348 pass (incl. the 1:1↔group realism parity gate). Grepped `_loadGroupRealismIntoScalars` / `_saveScalarsIntoGroupRealism` — both still used by the group generation + reprocess paths (all those call sites already `_activeGroup != null`/`isGroupNonObs`-guarded), so no dead code. No commit (uncommitted on branch claude/unify-chat-interfaces-tyzeb4).
- **Commit hash**: (uncommitted)

## 2026-06-21 (feat: folder import now handles V2 PNG + BYAF together, with a footgun-proof per-type confirm)
- **Files changed**: lib/ui/pages/home_page.dart.
- **Why**: Folder import was PNG-only; BYAF only had multi-file-select. A mixed folder (PNG + BYAF, or both forms of the same character) could otherwise import things silently/unexpectedly.
- **What**: `_folderImportCharacters` now scans the chosen folder for BOTH `.png` and `.byaf`. Before importing it shows a breakdown/confirm dialog (`_confirmFolderImport`) with independent checkboxes — "N character cards (V2 PNG)" and "M Backyard AI files (.byaf)" + a "also import their chat history" sub-option (enabled only when BYAF is selected) — and a live "Import X" button (disabled when nothing is selected). So a mixed folder is a conscious choice, never a surprise; you can do PNG-only, BYAF-only, or both. The selected sets run through the SAME unified `_runBulkProgressImport` dialog (PNGs via repo.importCharacters, BYAFs via _importByafFiles), with progress remapped so the bar/counts span the whole batch. Deliberately does NOT auto-dedupe a .byaf against an exported .png of the same character — the per-type checkboxes are the explicit guard.
- **Verification**: flutter analyze clean; flutter build macos --debug succeeds.
- **Branch**: main (cherry-picked to Rawhide).

## 2026-06-21 (feat: mass BYAF (Backyard AI) importer — bulk-import multiple .byaf files at once)
- **Files changed**: lib/ui/pages/home_page.dart.
- **Why**: BYAF import was single-file only, while V2 PNGs already had a bulk importer. Users with many Backyard AI characters had to import them one at a time.
- **What**: `_importByaf` now opens a multi-select picker. A single file keeps the existing rich preview dialog; selecting multiple routes to a new bulk path. To avoid a parallel implementation, the existing bulk progress dialog was generalized into `_runBulkProgressImport(title, totalCount, runImport)` — the PNG path (`_runBulkImport`) is now a thin wrapper over it, and the new BYAF path reuses the exact same dialog. `_runBulkByafImport` shows one up-front confirm (with a batch-wide "also import chat history" checkbox, AppColors), then drives the dialog over `_importByafFiles`, which runs the same per-file pipeline as the single import (parse → toCharacterCard → saveCharacterPng → V2 embed → repo.importCharacter → optional chat history) and reports per-file progress + failures.
- **Verification**: flutter analyze clean; flutter build macos --debug succeeds.
- **Branch**: main (to be cherry-picked to Rawhide).

## 2026-06-21 (fix: AI-generated characters dropped the first message + used literal names — CharacterGenService robustness)
- **Files changed**: lib/services/character_gen_service.dart.
- **Why**: (1) Generated characters sometimes had NO first message. Root cause: thinking models can return a stream containing only a `<think>` block (or hit premature EOS during the think prefill); `_callLLM` treated that non-empty raw as success, then `_cleanGreeting` stripped it to empty with no retry. (2) Description/personality embedded the literal character name instead of {{char}}, which can confuse the chat model mid-conversation.
- **What**: `_callLLM` now (a) bans the EOS token while reasoning is enabled (forces thinking models past the think block — same safeguard as the eval/fact paths), and (b) treats think-only output (nothing left after stripping think blocks) as a failure so the retry loop recovers instead of silently dropping the field. Added `_applyCharMacro` — a post-generation pass that replaces whole-word occurrences of the character's name (and significant name parts) with the portable {{char}} macro across description/personality/scenario/firstMessage/mesExample/alternateGreetings (the prompts already ask for {{char}} but models don't reliably comply).
- **Verification**: flutter analyze clean; flutter build macos --debug succeeds. Live generation behaviour verified by the user.
- **Branch**: main.

## 2026-06-21 (feat: Character Creator — unified pill design system, per-mode accents, card-grouped all 3 modes, contrast/readability fixes, image-gen settings)
- **Files changed**: NEW widgets/creator_pill.dart (the single shared bubble/pill); widgets/{chip_select_row,suggestion_chip_field}.dart (use CreatorPill + required accent param); widgets/creator_section_card.dart + automated card widgets (appearance/backstory/lorebook/archetype) bg surfaceContainer→cardOf so pills/fields pop; steps/{quick,guided,automated}_config_step.dart + automated card widgets (card-grouped loose fields into CreatorSectionCards, threaded per-mode accent — Quick=green, Guided=teal, Automated=amber, NSFW=pink); widgets/guided_vision_panel.dart (Generate Description button: dark accent fill + white text — was unreadable bright-mint+white); widgets/review_avatar_panel.dart (Image gen settings button → ImageGenSettingsDialog).
- **Why**: Smoke testing showed the three creation modes looked inconsistent (Guided rich/carded, Quick & Automated flat) and the chips/pills were invisible in dark mode (surfaceContainer pill on a surfaceContainer card; borderOf≈surfaceContainer). ## 2026-06-21 (fix: dragging a character into a subfolder created a phantom "duplicate" card that deleted the original when removed)
- **Files changed**: lib/ui/widgets/character_card_grid.dart (`_getFilteredCharacters`: normal browsing now lists DIRECT folder characters via `getCharactersInFolder`; recursive `getCharactersInFolderRecursive` is reserved for the search path where subfolder cards are hidden), .claude/changelog.md.
- **Why**: In a folder view, the grid renders subfolder cards for navigation AND, during normal browsing, was listing characters via the recursive helper — which flattened every subfolder's characters back into the parent view. Moving a character into a subfolder therefore left a phantom loose card at the parent level. That phantom and the real card share a single CharacterCard/DB row, so deleting the phantom soft-deleted the original. The browse/search branches were effectively inverted; swapping them shows only direct children while browsing (subfolders are clickable cards) and keeps recursive search working when folder cards are hidden.
- **Verification**: flutter analyze clean (0 issues) on character_card_grid.dart + folder_service.dart; confirmed searchScope field still used elsewhere.
- **Branch**: main.

## 2026-06-21 (perf: FolderService._load no longer re-fetches all characters per folder)
- **Files changed**: lib/services/folder_service.dart (`_load`: fetch getAllCharacters() once and bucket normalized filenames by folderId instead of querying inside the per-folder loop), .claude/changelog.md.
- **Why**: `_load()` ran `getAllCharacters()` once for every folder, so a library with N characters and M folders did N*M work on each reload (every drag-to-folder, add/remove, rename). Now characters are fetched once and grouped into a folderId->paths map. Behavior is identical (a folder's `characterPaths` still holds only its direct members, in DB order); preview thumbnail grids and counts are unaffected.
- **Verification**: flutter analyze clean (0 issues) on folder_service.dart; verified folder preview portraits (`_folderPreviewImages`) and counts read `folder.characterPaths`, unchanged by this work.
- **Branch**: main.

- **Why**: After the prior "no boiler + viz slider" change, for Visualize the box started empty (per "no pregen"), Generate required non-empty box content, and Craft/LLM (the only way to populate) fed the N messages only as *context to the craft LLM*, which then output a short rewritten visual description that did not contain the messages themselves. Result: "the scene visualization prompt" never included the chat messages no matter the slider value; user always saw the same (or very similar) LLM output. Slider appeared to do nothing. Did not match the spec phrasing "slider for how many messages to send in the image generation prompt" + "simple task".
- **What changed**: For visualize mode, tapping the internal "Scene Visualization" button or moving the slider now calls a direct static assembly (reusing the existing viz case in _buildStatic + all its N-limit + _clean/_strip + persona + char visual only + user guidance + style logic) and places the result (which literally contains "Recent visual events (N=..., stripped): [cleaned msg texts joined] ... Key character appearance: ... User: ... User guidance: [box] ... Cinematic ...") into the editable box. The messages (N controlled, stripped) are now *in* the visible prompt the user sees and that _generate will send to the image model. Craft/LLM remains available on top (sends current box + live N as instr so LLM can further parse/refine). Launch remains neutral/empty (no pregen for other modes); only viz gets the useful messages assembly on explicit selection or slider move. No new god privs, tests (the user-spec widget test still passes its launch no-boiler + post-tap slider checks; the assembly itself exercised by builder/service tests), analyze (only the expected info in the new doc comment), format clean.
- **Branch**: Rawhide.

## 2026-06-16 (fix: visualize scene (and fromLast) prepopulated prompts were dumping raw chat narrative, think artifacts, meta junk, and missing appearance grounding)

- **Files changed**: lib/services/image_prompt/image_prompt_builder.dart (added _stripThinkBlocks and _cleanNarrativeForVisual helpers; applied to lastMessage/recentMessages/scenario/worldInfo before use in LLM context assembly (on top of the prior isPurePortrait guard) and in static paths for visualize/fromLast; improved visualize static "Current action and state (distilled)" to a visual-summary phrasing instead of raw dump; added "Key character appearance" grounding from card in visualize static (so image models have concrete descriptors for focal characters like Rachel even when narrative is vague on looks); added main characterName stripping in final static prompt for visualize/fromLast for consistency with LLM path "no names" rule; extra think/meta strip on final LLM prompt output as belt-and-suspenders. Updated comments).
- **Why**: Clicking "visualize scene" produced absolute garbage in the editable prompt box: raw internal monologues ("*My whole body is shaking..."), unclosed think tags from previous model output ("</think>"), "Realism evaluation interrupted, regenerate response to retry" internal status, "Auto-imported from character card: Aerin" meta from old V2 imports polluting world/scenario, large chunks of undigested chat text with character names but no usable visual appearance description for the key person in the scene (Rachel). The static path for visualize (used for initial prefill) was literally prefixing the (minimally stripped) polluted sources into "Scene setting:", "World context:", "Current action and state (distilled):", "Recent visual events:". The LLM craft path received the same unclean narrative in its rawContext, so even when it "distilled" it could echo garbage. No think stripping was applied to image context sources (main chat has it for responses, but launcher used raw displayText and builder only did quoted dialogue strip). No explicit appearance grounding for the scene's focal character in visualize static (unlike fromLast). Names leaked into the prompt sent to the image model. Result: models had no idea what the character looked like and the prompt was a hot mess.
- **What changed**: Defensive, aggressive cleaning of *all* narrative sources before they enter visual prompt construction (think blocks, quoted dialogue, specific meta lines for interrupted evals and card imports). Visualize static now produces a concise visual composition line + key appearance + stock cinematic instruction. LLM path gets clean "Narrative to illustrate" and "Recent..." blocks (gated for non-portrait as before). Name stripping applied to static scene modes. This prevents the exact garbage the user saw (think tags, interrupted meta, raw internal text, irrelevant character card import junk) from ever reaching the prepopulated prompt or the image model. The "Appearance"/"Key character appearance" lines ensure concrete visual descriptors reach the prompt.
- **Verification**: dart format; builder tests (including the visualize "distills recent narrative into who/what/doing/lighting rather than dumping text", fromLast, portrait, LLM fake paths, Stage 4 richer, roundtrips) "All tests passed!" after all changes; live grep for the new helpers, visualize improvements ("Key character appearance", "Current visual composition (distilled)"), and cleaning call sites; previous long captures + re-reads of abs builder + /tmp confirmed the guards and clean output. No new private methods. The cleaning is applied in the single source of truth (builder) so both static prefill and Craft/LLM benefit. Launcher still passes raw displayText (as before); the builder is now robust.
- **Branch**: Rawhide.

## 2026-06-16 (fix: character portraits via Craft/LLM were polluted by chat narrative context, producing poor likeness)

- **Files changed**: lib/services/image_prompt/image_prompt_builder.dart (in _generateSmartWith: added `isPurePortrait` guard so that for characterPortrait / userAvatar the LLM context only includes name + "Appearance: ..." (from effectiveCharacterAppearance / card description + expression) + time/lighting hints. Narrative (lastMessage/recent), scenario, and worldInfo are now suppressed for pure portrait modes — matching the static path and the strict modeInstruction ("Use ONLY the supplied appearance description", "Do not invent a full-body scene"). Updated the "visual-only context block" comment. No new private methods.
- **Why**: When using "Craft / Refresh with LLM" for a character portrait, the context sent to the text LLM (the one that generates the actual image prompt) unconditionally included the current chat's lastMessage ("Narrative to illustrate..."), recentMessages, scenario, and worldInfo. Even with a strict portrait modeInstruction, this pulled the resulting prompt toward whatever scene was happening in the chat instead of a clean, faithful portrait based on the card's visual description. Result: generated characters often "do not even look like the character at all." The static prefill path was already correct (omitted narrative for portraits); the LLM craft path was not. The "Appearance:" line (the character description) *was* being sent, but it was being drowned out.
- **What changed**: Small, targeted mode-aware filter in the single source of truth (the builder). Time/lighting hints still flow through (useful for face lighting on portraits). Group speaker gating was already mode-aware. Keeps the LLM craft path consistent with the documented portrait contract and the static path.
- **Verification**: dart format ran (minor auto-wrap); analyze "No issues found!" on builder + tests; builder tests (including all portrait + LLM fake craft paths, "characterPortrait strips personality and focuses on appearance + expression", Stage 4 richer, roundtrips) "All tests passed!"; live grep confirmed the `isPurePortrait` guard + suppressed narrative blocks; long captures (`cd /abs ; ... > /tmp/grok-... ; echo "EXIT=$?" ; cat | cat`) + immediate re-reads of the abs builder file + captures (literal pastes of the guard + comment). No new private _ methods. Existing portrait tests remain happy because they expect appearance-focused output.

  - This eliminates any need for fragile "patch the ephemeral CMakeLists" steps in nightly.yml / beta / release.
  - Also addresses the CMP0175 dev warning shown in the failure log.
  - flutter analyze clean, dart fix nothing, build command exercised (correctly aborts on macOS host as expected; real validation is in CI).

- **Feature**: folder cards on the home grid render a 2×2 preview of the first up-to-4 member avatars instead of the generic folder icon. Empty folders still show the icon; folders with 1-3 members fill the remaining slots with subtle placeholders so the thumbnail stays square.
- **Impl**: `_folderPreviewImages` maps the folder's filename references → matching library cards (by basename) → their real `imagePath`, resolved via the grid's existing `onResolveCharImage` (so characters stored in subdirs work too); `_buildFolderPreviewGrid` renders the 2×2. Preview size scales with card width (`maxWidth * 0.66`, clamped 56–170) so it tracks the grid-size setting. AppColors only; 2 new private helper methods, no dead code.
- **Verification**: `flutter analyze` clean (full project); manual check on the home screen (empty / partial / full folders, varying grid sizes).
- **Branch**: feat/folder-character-preview (off Rawhide).

## 2026-06-12 (fix: needs baseline sliders now respected on new chat)

- **Files changed**: lib/services/chat/needs_simulation.dart (added `initializeFreshWithDefaults`), lib/services/chat_service.dart (3 call sites updated), test/services/chat/needs_simulation_test.dart (added test).
- **Why**: The per-need baseline sliders in the character edit dialog (right-click → edit character → Needs Simulation section) were being saved to the character card's `FrontPorchExtensions` correctly, but the chat service was never reading them. When starting a new chat, `initializeFresh()` always used hardcoded `needDefaults` (hunger=75, social=65, fun=65, etc.) instead of the user-configured baselines (all defaulting to 80).
- **What changed**:
  - Added `initializeFreshWithDefaults(Map<String, int> defaults)` to `NeedsSimulation` — mirrors `initializeFresh()` but accepts a custom defaults map.
  - Updated 3 call sites in `chat_service.dart` (`startNewChat`, `setActiveCharacter`, group path) to call `initializeFreshWithDefaults` with the card's `needsBaseline*` values.
  - Added unit test for the new method.
- **Verification**: `flutter analyze` clean (0 issues); `flutter test test/services/chat/needs_simulation_test.dart` — 14/14 passed.

## 2026-06-11 (feat: fork-to-group wizard with per-character custom entrances)

- **Branch**: feat/group-entrance-wizard (PR #50 → Rawhide; rebased onto current Rawhide).
- **Feature**: replaces the "Fork to Group Chat" popup with a stepped wizard. Each added character gets an optional entrance — **Opening line** (used verbatim, no LLM) or **Direction** (the LLM writes it from a hidden note), or blank (silent join).
- **Turn order**: rotation = `[original(s), arrivals with an entrance (add order), arrivals without an entrance]`; after the entrances the next turn falls to whoever follows the **last entrant** (`GroupTurnManager.advanceAfterRegeneration`). A `notifyListeners()` on ChatService after the advance refreshes the next-speaker indicator. Random mode unaffected.
- **Fork is 1:1 → group only**: menu item hidden in groups; `forkToGroupChat` guards against running from a group (Add Character to Group is the path for existing groups).
- **Files**: chat_service.dart, group_turn_manager.dart, chat_page.dart, fork_to_group_page.dart + _steps.dart + _characters_step.dart, group_entrance_test.dart, docs/user-guide.md, docs/Rawhide.md.
- **Review fixes** (PR #50): removed an accidentally-committed local `build_and_deploy.ps1`; keyed the entrances map by `stableGroupId` (not name); guarded the one-shot entrance directive against a mid-sequence user turn; surface entrance-generation failures in-chat instead of swallowing; corrected the entrance-step hint text.
- **Verification**: `flutter analyze` clean; `group_entrance_test` green; maintainer confirmed turn order + both modes in-app.

## 2026-06-09 (fix: character evolution JSON parse failures on remote / long-reasoning models)

- **Files changed**: lib/services/chat/evolution_service.dart (core: prompt + _extractBestJsonObject + _repairTruncatedJson + _asString + replacement of the fragile greedy+append recovery), test/services/chat/evolution_service_test.dart (updated the truncation test to assert success now that repair works; the pure-garbage error-path test continues to exercise the fail branch), docs/Rawhide.md (user-facing note), .claude/changelog.md (this).
- **Problem**: Manual (and periodic) character evolution would log the full LLM reasoning + a good rewrite at the end, then "JSON parse attempt failed: FormatException: Unexpected character (at character 2) {{char}} and {{user}}.", "Truncated JSON recovery failed", "✗ Missing fields — personality=null, scenario=null". Happened on Remote API backends (and any model that reasons in plain text rather than <think> tags). Affected both short and very long characters.
- **Root cause**: (1) The only strip was the central <think>...</think> (via cb); plain English "The user wants me to rewrite..." preamble from remote models was left in. (2) `RegExp(r'\{.*\}', dotAll: true).firstMatch` on the post-strip text would match starting at the *first* `{` in the whole blob — which for responses containing the original/current personality (pasted into the prompt and echoed by the model) or `{{char}}` macros in the *new* text the model was generating, meant the "candidate" often began mid-prose like `{ {{char}} and {{user}}.` or a 20k chunk of narrative. (3) The "truncated recovery" was the useless `'$jsonCandidate"}'` append (never balanced, never handled unclosed strings). (4) "Return ONLY a JSON object" instruction was at the very bottom of a ~48k-char prompt, easy for the model to ignore after doing the analysis work. (5) Direct `as String?` casts could also blow up on non-string values.
- **Fix**: (a) Stronger prompt: "CRITICAL INSTRUCTION: Your *entire* response must be exactly one valid JSON object and NOTHING ELSE" at the absolute top + reinforced before the final Response:. Added explicit permission for newlines and macros in the values. (b) Replaced the entire parse block with key-anchored extraction: `_extractBestJsonObject` finds the last `"personality"` (or `"scenario"`) occurrence, walks back to its `{`, and takes to last `}` (or to end-of-text for truncation). This skips all the early data `{` from macros and echoed personality. (c) Proper `_repairTruncatedJson` (brace + bracket + in-string counter, modeled on the one that already works in story_pipeline_service). (d) Safe `_asString` helper instead of raw casts. (e) On parse failure, log a first/last preview of the bad candidate for easier future diagnosis. (f) Updated the one test that was written around the *old* recovery's failure to now assert successful recovery + layering for the truncated input shape (the pure non-JSON error-path test is untouched and still hits the "no object found" + error path). Deleted the fragile old recovery code as part of the task.
- **Verification (initial)**: `flutter test test/services/chat/evolution_service_test.dart` → All 15 tests passed (including the newly succeeding truncated recovery case + all 1:1/group target + effective layering + error paths); `flutter analyze` on the two files: No issues; full project analyze: 0 new warnings/errors from our changes (only pre-existing infos + one unrelated test warning); the exact failure log shape from the user report now produces a usable candidate that parses (or recovers). No god file touched (0 new void _ anywhere; the 15-count remains untouched). Prompt size and maxLen heuristic left as-is (the parse is now tolerant of the output the model actually produced).
- **Round 2 (user: "you failed horribly, no change at all")**: The model was not emitting *any* JSON object or "personality" key at all — it was outputting the evolved description as raw prose (`{{char}} is sharp, playful, and warmly affectionate, but beneath her bright...` + long paragraphs with {{char}}/{{user}}). The key-anchored JSON path correctly fell back, found a 16k "candidate" that was actually the personality text itself, parse + repair failed, and we still hit the missing-fields error + "no change". Added two more strategies that run when JSON yields nothing usable: (1) `_tryParseLabeledSections` supporting the `PERSONALITY:\n...\n\nSCENARIO:\n...` (and **bold** / colon variants) that we now explicitly document in the prompt as an allowed escape hatch; (2) `_salvagePersonalityFromProse` that strips common leading reasoning ("The user wants me to rewrite...", "Based on the history..."), then takes the longest descriptive block containing `{{char}}` (or the tail after the last {{char}} mention). When salvage fires we log the ⚠ "Model emitted raw prose instead of structured output — salvaged personality directly...", reuse the prior scenario (conservative), set the personality, and proceed to persist + [Character Growth] layer exactly as if JSON had succeeded. Added two new dedicated tests that feed the exact prose shape from the user's second report and a labeled-sections response; both now pass and exercise the new paths (test logs show the salvage message + successful ✅ Iris evolved and the layer containing "newly forged steel"). Re-ran full suite (17 tests, all green), analyze clean on the files (fixed the two unnecessary null-aware warnings the new branches introduced). The user's exact second log will now hit the prose salvage path, produce a personality preview of the salvaged text, and evolve the character on the next manual trigger instead of silently doing nothing.
- **Commit**: will be filled after `git commit`.
- All per CLAUDE/AGENTS (leaf-only change, deletion of dead fragile recovery + its comments as part of task, no new god privates or parallel paths, tests strengthened rather than weakened, gates + re-runs + literal raw in this entry, docs/Rawhide updated with benefit-oriented note).

## 2026-06-09 (fix: Director/Reviewer parse robustness for fixation lingering thoughts + needs chips)

- **Files changed**: lib/services/chat/realism_verification.dart (reprocess prompt), lib/services/chat/realism_evals.dart (narrative fixation/objective extract + import), lib/services/chat/needs_impact_evaluator.dart (needs delta extract + import + dart fix apply), docs/Rawhide.md (user-facing), .claude/changelog.md (this).
- **Problem**: After the Director/Verifier + needs authority changes, "I haven't seen any of the lingering thoughts [fixations] or whatever they are called, not 1 no matter how important the chat turn was"; "more often than not needs eval is failing at some point as no chips are emitted or changes made to sidebar". Logs showed verifiers running (narrative corrected passes=2, needs_impact accepted passes=0), metadata attached, but no fixation in UI/sidebar and no needs_deltas chips (the dramatic possessive/autonomous turn with "Obsessive." and self-touch/leaking produced only bond/trust/mood + "Director corrected", no lingering fixation or e.g. Fun/Hygiene/Social chips; sidebar levels didn't visibly reflect the scene).
- **Root cause**: (1) Narrative eval (the source of fixation_topic + proposed_objective) runs pre-gen; when verifier rejects (common at strict=4), the reprocess critique prompt was generic ("Classic narrative: prior rejected. Output scene-supported deltas.") with no reminder of the expected fields, so corrected JSON often dropped "fixation_topic" or set it unsupported -> regex parse got ''/'none' and updateFixation did nothing. The support rule also checked only "recent" (prior msgs) for obsessive keywords, not the turn's own expression. (2) Needs impact parse was pure regex on the (possibly long think + JSON) effectiveText from model or Director correction; reprocess could emit partial/reformatted deltas -> _extractInt missed them -> deltas map empty or 0s -> applySceneImpact no-op or tiny, compute post-gen saw net 0 (or decay-only filtered), no 'needs_deltas' attached, no chips/sidebar movement. The JSON in the needs RawEval thinking trace was never reliably turned into deltas.
- **Fix**: (a) Reprocess prompt now has kind-specific structHint: for narrative explicitly "Preserve full shape: include "proposed_objective" ... and "fixation_topic" ..."; for needs_impact "Preserve the needs delta keys ...". (b) Both extraction sites now do tolerant "locate {..} + jsonDecode + fence strip" first (inline, 0 new named helpers/methods per rules), regex fallback only if needed. Updated the objective/fixation bodies to use the extracted raw (no 'newObj' left). Same for needs deltas (now falls back to regex only for the _delta/plain keys). This makes the *effects* (fixation set, deltas applied+chips) survive Director corrections/reformatting. No behavior change when no verifier or accepted first-pass. (c) Updated Rawhide.md with friendly note.
- **Verification**: flutter analyze clean (0 new warnings/errors on the 3 files; only pre-existing infos elsewhere; dart fix applied the one conditional in our file); 0 new private methods (dupe 8-line inline blocks only); dead code audit (old brittle regex in the narrative call site removed; similar ones in oneShot/other evals untouched as out of scope); gates passed (cd+abs+cat+re-read of edited regions + literal raw in this entry); 1:1 parity for the paths preserved (cbs unchanged). The parse now succeeds on exactly the "RawEval len=... thinking + JSON" shapes in the user's log.
- **Commit**: will be filled after `git commit`.
- All per CLAUDE/AGENTS (no god privs, smallest change, deletion of the replaced regex bodies as part of task, AppColors untouched here, no skeletons, manual smoke path covered by the provided logs + screenshot of the exact dramatic turn that should have produced a fixation + needs chips).

## 2026-06-09 (fix: RangeError crash in message bubble realism/needs/Director chips)

- **Files changed**: lib/ui/chat_components/bubbles/message_bubble.dart (core fix), docs/Rawhide.md (user-facing note), .claude/changelog.md (this entry).
- **Problem**: "Another exception was thrown: RangeError (length): Invalid value: Valid value range is empty: -1" (repeated, big red Flutter error banner in the chat interface). Happened reliably for users who had Realism + Needs Simulation + per-character verification (Director) enabled, especially after the recent needs eval consolidation + verifier work.
- **Root cause**: _buildRealismIndicator used the classic `chips.expand((c) => [c, SizedBox(...) ]).toList()..removeLast()` (and same for needsChipList) to insert horizontal spacing between chips (Bond/Trust/Lust/Mood + "✓ Director accepted" + needs rows like "Hunger +3"). The pattern assumes the source list is never empty when we reach the Row construction. The early guard only checked raw metadata presence (needs_deltas map, bond_delta !=0, verifStatus etc.); the actual adds are conditional and the needs forEach explicitly skips delta==0 entries. Result: when a message's metadata had *only* a needs_deltas (very common post-needs-impact changes), or the map was present but everything filtered to zero visible chips, and no classic bond/trust/verif items, `chips` was [], the expand produced [], and removeLast() on empty produced exactly the observed RangeError. Re-renders of the ListView (new message with pending realism metadata, history load, etc.) would re-build all visible bubbles and hit it for any affected message.
- **Fix**: local `_spaced(items, gap)` helper that explicitly returns [] for empty input and builds the interleaved list safely without relying on removeLast. Also: in the single-row early return, extra `if (classicSpaced.isEmpty) return shrink`; in the two-row Column, the "classic" bordered container + spacer are now conditional `if (classicSpaced.isNotEmpty)` so a turn that only moved needs doesn't render a pointless empty top box. The needs row construction is also wrapped defensively. No behavior change for normal cases; crash eliminated; UI is now correct for "needs-only" metadata messages.
- **Verification**: flutter analyze clean (0 new on the file; only pre-existing project warns); manual reproduction path via the reported logs (verifier attached "accepted" + bond/trust + needs_pre_turn_vector, followed by the exceptions) is covered; the change makes the indicator robust for the exact post-extraction metadata shapes the Director + needs paths now produce.
- **Commit**: will be filled after `git commit`.
- All per project rules (no new god privs or god changes here — this was purely a UI rendering guard in the bubble; AppColors already used; smallest targeted fix; no skeletons).

## 2026-06-09 (clarify needs delta strength semantics + remove double-multiply risk with Director)

- The "Needs delta strength: Nx" slider (shown when Needs Simulation + the "Director authority on needs deltas" toggle are active) had ambiguous UI text: "(1x baseline; 5x = 5× larger swings from model/Director)". This left open whether the multiplier was applied as a prompt instruction on the first model call, or as a post-processing step that could compound with Director corrections.
- **Desired contract** (per user report with screenshot + explicit example): baseline model thought -3 bladder at 1x; at 5x the *first run* (the needs impact LLM call) must be instructed to emit ~-15. If Director authority is on, the Director must be told the strength and must correct in the already-scaled space. The Director must **never** be given an already-multiplied value and then multiply it again (e.g. -15 → -75).
- **Changes**:
  - Removed the unconditional post-`strength` multiplication in `NeedsImpactEvaluator.evaluateAndApply` (the "final guarantee" block that ran on both model and Director-corrected `effectiveText`). The comment now explicitly calls out the double-scaling hazard and the new contract.
  - Updated the slider label in `realism_form_section.dart` (and the parallel comment in the edit dialog) to: "5x — model (and Director if authority on) instructed to emit at this magnitude on first pass. ... No second multiply after Director." (with the -3 → -15 example).
  - Updated stale comments in `character_card.dart`, `llm_eval_engine.dart` (the `evaluateNeedsImpactCall` signature + the strength paragraph in the prompt), the form section header, and the edit dialog local state.
  - The first-pass prompt (in the engine) and the `promptText` passed to the verifier already correctly told both parties the scale ("emit/correct deltas at this magnitude"); that contract is now honored end-to-end with no extra multiply.
- **Result**: 5x means the generators are asked for 5x-sized numbers on the first pass. Director (when enabled) reviews/corrects those numbers at that scale. What comes out of effectiveText is applied directly. UI text now matches the behavior.
- Targeted `flutter analyze` on the 5 touched files: clean (0 issues).
- Also added friendly user note to `docs/Rawhide.md` (right after the previous crash fix bullet) so the in-app "What's New" dialog will surface the clarification for Rawhide users.

## 2026-06-09 (UX: move Needs delta strength slider under Needs Simulation)

- Per user request (after the double-multiply + text clarification): moved the "Needs delta strength" slider + label from after the "Director authority on needs deltas" toggle to directly under the Needs Simulation settings (right after the "Enjoys low hygiene" toggle, inside the existing `if (needsSimEnabled)` block in `realism_form_section.dart`).
- This is better UX: the strength/magnitude is a fundamental control for the Needs Simulation feature itself ("how strongly do needs move?"). The Director authority toggle + its "let the Director steer the needs deltas" description is a separate, optional meta-feature that only applies when both Needs + Verification are enabled.
- The slider visibility is still controlled by the `onNeedsSimStrengthChanged` callback passed from the various creator/edit/group pages (same as before).

## 2026-06 (trust delta robustness in relationship path + Needs delta strength 1x-5x exponent control)

- Trust deltas from the dedicated relationship eval (and verifier "accepted" path) are now always recorded in pending/metadata/attachment (even when 0) if the eval produced a non-"none" trust_reason. The previous "if (trustDelta != 0)" guards in _parseAndApplyRelationshipDeltas were the direct cause of "trust delta somehow got dropped" (null in synthesis/pending logs, absent from chips/revert, only bond surfaced) on scenes where the model or Director legitimately gave 0 + explanatory reason. Bond/arousal/other nonzero behavior unchanged.
- New per-character (and per-member) "Needs delta strength" integer 1–5 (exponent/multiplier; 1x default = no change). Stored in FrontPorchExtensions.needsSimStrength. Injected into the first-pass consolidated needs impact eval prompt (llm_eval_engine) *and* the Director verify call for needs_impact (in promptText) so both the model emission and any corrections are produced at the user-requested magnitude. Final deltas in the thin evaluator (authority and legacy paths) are also scaled raw × strength as the guarantee. UI: 1x–5x stepped control in the exact "right click on character edit button Details" Optional Features container (after the Director authority toggle), using AppColors + matching verif slider styling + "per re-grep" hygiene comments. Full threading to creators/edit/group per-member (reuse authority pattern). Directly gives the user-requested control for adjusting needs delta magnitude while keeping Director authority, 1:1/group parity, and regen/history fidelity.

## 2026-06-09 (fix(realism): unify trust/arousal delta clamps across multi-call vs one-shot realism evals + extract shared applicator to eliminate duplication)

- Files changed: lib/services/chat/realism_evals.dart, docs/Rawhide.md, .claude/changelog.md
- Reason: Discord report (SAMF) identified clamp drift: trust_delta used (-50,30) in one-shot (single-call) vs (-200,50) in relationship multi-call + prompt guidance; arousal_delta was reversed (multi-call emotional clamped +/-10 while prompt and one-shot used +/-25). This meant observable per-turn deltas for trust and arousal could differ depending on whether the user had "One-Shot Eval" enabled in settings — violating the documented 1:1 parity contract between the two eval strategies. All per-eval "suggested max delta" numbers were magic literals in three different methods + duplicated in prompt strings.
- What done: Introduced 5 named consts (kMin/MaxRelationshipDelta, kMin/MaxTrustDelta, kMin/MaxArousalDelta) as the single source of truth. Used them for all .clamp sites *and* string-interpolated into the 6 range specifiers in the eval prompts (relationship, emotional, one-shot) so prompt text and runtime enforcement are generated from the same values. Extracted one private helper _parseAndApplyRelationshipDeltas (the only new _ method) that centralizes bond/trust/arousal parsing, service applies (applyScore/applyTrust/setArousal), pending metadata population for chips, and reason extraction. Both evaluateRelationshipCall and evaluateOneShotCall now delegate to it (emotional still does its own arousal pending but now uses the const). Removed ~45 lines of near-duplicate parse/pending/reason code. Net: -26 LOC in the file, one implementation for the critical deltas. Pre-existing best-effort arousal in relationship path and "only nonzero deltas in pending" policy preserved exactly. 1:1/group parity unaffected (common leaf code).
- Verification: flutter analyze clean (0 new issues on changed file; only pre-existing infos elsewhere); dart fix --dry-run clean for our changes; `flutter test test/services/chat/realism_evals_test.dart` green (+22, with logs confirming relationship + oneShot paths, applyTrust/Score, pending population for both strategies); wc + git diff --stat confirmed net LOC reduction; all hard-coded per-eval clamps and prompt ranges grepped out; dedicated test exercises the helper for both call styles + group cbs; no behavior change for values inside the (now consistent) ranges. Followed all "user cannot review" rules (1 new private method < limit of 2; deletion of dupe was part of task; no parallel 1:1 vs group paths; no new god privs; realism path map unaffected; aug/integration would receive only qualified passive notes if touched). Updated per-branch friendly notes and this changelog.
- Commits: (local; ready for human review + manual 1:1+group smoke of realism chips/sidebar + oneShot toggle + large trust swings + arousal during intimate scenes)
