2026-06-22 (UTC) — Scene Guests: harden guest-resolution against concurrent/torn-down DB access (crash hardening)
Files changed: lib/services/chat_service.dart (_resolveSceneGuestCards re-entrancy guard + disposed checks; _onCharacterLibraryChanged defers + guards), .claude/changelog.md.
Brief reason: App crashed with a native SQLite use-after-free (Thread 14: sqlite3 vdbeUnbind/bindText, pc=0x0) on a DartWorker — the signature of the VM/native resources being reinitialized while a DB op was in flight, almost certainly a hot reload/restart triggered by editing .dart files during a live `flutter run -d macos` session. Independent of that tooling cause, the recently-added _onCharacterLibraryChanged listener (re-resolves scene guests on every CharacterRepository change) did synchronous DB reads from inside the repo's notify callback with no re-entrancy guard — a real concurrency risk. Hardened: (1) _resolveSceneGuestCards now guards against overlapping passes (one runs at a time; concurrent requests coalesce into a single trailing re-run via _resolvingSceneGuests/_sceneGuestsResolvePending) so two passes can never race the per-id DB reads or the shared id/card list mutation, and bails on _disposed mid-pass (never touches the DB after teardown); (2) _onCharacterLibraryChanged now skips when _disposed/_guestBusy/no-guests and defers the resolve via scheduleMicrotask so it never starts a read from inside the repository's in-progress write/notify, re-checking guards on the microtask. The deferred listener resolve also won't fight the create/enter flow (which sets _guestBusy and owns its own resolve). NOTE: the disposed guards don't fully prevent a hot-restart-mid-DB-op crash (the old isolate is discarded without a clean dispose) — that's a dev-workflow issue (don't edit Dart against a live flutter run); these guards remove the in-app concurrency risk. flutter analyze clean; 1292 tests pass; flutter build macos --debug green. Not committed.

2026-06-22 (UTC) — Scene Guests: hardening pass from a 4-reviewer adversarial audit (concurrency / parity / generation / UI)
Files changed: lib/services/chat_service.dart, lib/services/chat/scene_guest_director.dart, lib/services/chat/cast_detector.dart, lib/services/chat/scene_guest_factory.dart, lib/services/chat/chat_command_handler.dart, lib/ui/pages/chat_page.dart, lib/ui/widgets/character_card_grid.dart, test/services/chat/cast_detector_test.dart (+5), test/services/chat/scene_guest_director_test.dart (+3), .claude/changelog.md.
Brief reason: Ran four parallel hostile reviewers over the whole Scene Guests surface; verified each finding against the code and fixed the real ones.
CONTEXT-TOKEN SAFETY (crash class): added _sceneChanged(token) guard (snapshots _currentSessionId) and threaded it through every fire-and-forget guest op so a chat switch / dispose between awaits can't write the wrong chat: _resolveSceneGuestCards (per-id + pre-writeback), _onCharacterLibraryChanged microtask, _performCastScan (no stale popup in the wrong chat), _addGuestWithStatus (mint/enter/status/portrait), _maybeGenerateGuestPortrait (skip if guest left / chat switched + unique per-invocation temp filename), and the chime-in director (new isContextValid bail between guests). This closes the in-app window behind the earlier SQLite use-after-free.
HOST-INVARIANT (parity): (1) _sceneGuestForMessage now keys off _isGuestAuthoredMessage (stable characterId vs the host's), removing the name-fallback that could misclassify a host message as a guest's on a name collision; (2) regenerating a DEPARTED guest's message is now refused (was running the full host realism revert+re-eval against guest-authored text — a real host bond/trust/emotion/needs perturbation); swipe uses the same authoritative check; (3) loadSession (history switch) now resets + reloads scene-guest state for 1:1 (was leaking the previous session's guests into and contaminating the loaded session's blob); (4) STOPPED mutating the shared library card — the scenario auto-repair wrote card.scenario='' on the repo's live reference (corrupting a /join'd character for when it's a host); the guest scenario is now blanked ONLY in the prompt at guest-turn time (still self-heals legacy guests, preserves real scenarios); (5) continueGeneration + impersonateUser now guard _guestBusy.
GENERATION/DETECTION: cast_detector JSON parse switched from greedy \{.*\} (died on trailing prose / two objects) to a balanced brace-scan _firstJsonObject; _collides is token-aware (≥3-char non-title shared token) so "Ed" no longer suppresses "Fred"/"Ned" and "Sam"≠"Samuel", while "Mara"/"Mara Vance" still collide; cast scan reads HOST-authored narration only (excludes guest messages); _buildGuestGrounding skips grounding when the guest's first name overlaps the host/user (host-bleed); director nickname heuristic ignores title first-tokens ("Major Tom" no longer fires on "major"); factory safeName falls back to 'guest' for non-Latin/symbol names.
UX/MISC: _addGuestWithStatus rejects a duplicate guest name and surfaces "busy" instead of silently dropping; _maybeEvolveGuest persists the bumped participation count on non-evolving turns; a deleted/departed guest's old bubble now shows a placeholder avatar (not the host's face); /exit with an ambiguous substring asks for the full name instead of removing the first match; Scene Guests get a "Guest" badge in the library grid (uses the previously-dead isLite getter; they stay visible so they remain deletable / known-cast). Verified: flutter analyze clean, 1299 tests pass (7 new), flutter build macos --debug green.
KNOWN FOLLOW-UPS (not blockers): chat_service.dart grew across this work and should have the scene-guest session/persistence/portrait orchestration extracted into a chat/scene_guest_session.dart leaf; guest regen intentionally does not re-advance evolution/memory (a swipe replaces a turn); forkFromMessage intentionally inherits guests; the error-state banner reuses the existing Colors.orangeAccent accent (matches the trust-repair banner).

2026-06-22 (UTC) — Scene Guests: guest messages no longer inherit the host's "✓ Director accepted" chip
Files changed: lib/services/chat_service.dart (_generateResponse new-message metadata), .claude/changelog.md.
Brief reason: User saw a "✓ Director accepted" realism-verification chip on guest bubbles, though guests run no realism. Root cause: the HOST turn's post-gen realism verification stashes its result into the shared _pendingRealismMetadata (realism_evals.applyBatchResults → setPendingRealismMetadata, key RealismVerification.kMetaKey) for the god to stamp onto the host message. That field persisted into the subsequent chime-in, and the guest turn's new-message creation in _generateResponse attached _pendingRealismMetadata verbatim — so the guest bubble inherited the host's verification chip (and any leftover bond/emotion deltas). Fix: when guestSpeaker != null, the new message's initialMetadata is forced to null (guests carry zero Realism/Needs metadata). The host path (guestSpeaker == null) is byte-for-byte unchanged, so host chips are unaffected; the existing _pendingRealismMetadata = null after message creation still clears it so nothing bleeds onward. flutter analyze clean; 1299 tests pass; flutter build macos --debug green.

2026-06-22 (UTC) — Scene Guests: "type /" slash-command helper panel (command discovery)
Files changed: lib/services/chat/chat_command_handler.dart (new SlashCommandInfo + static ChatCommandHandler.commands registry), lib/ui/pages/chat_page.dart (import + _buildCommandHelper + ValueListenableBuilder panel in _buildInputArea), test/services/chat/chat_command_handler_test.dart (+1 drift guard), docs/Rawhide.md, .claude/changelog.md.
Brief reason: Users had no way to discover the slash commands. Added an inline command list that appears above the input the moment the text is a command-in-progress (regex ^/(\w*)$ — so it shows on "/", "/cr", … and hides once a space/args are typed), filtered by the typed prefix; tapping a row fills the input with "/command " and keeps focus to continue typing args. SINGLE SOURCE OF TRUTH: a static const ChatCommandHandler.commands list (SlashCommandInfo{command, example, description}) drives the panel so it can't drift from the handler; a new test asserts every advertised command is actually recognized by handle(). The panel is rendered IN the input column (like the existing status/trust banners — no OverlayEntry / manual positioning, sidestepping the fragile parts of autocomplete) and scoped to the controller via ValueListenableBuilder<TextEditingValue> so only the panel rebuilds per keystroke (not the whole page). AppColors-clean (surfaceContainer/border/relationshipAccent/textSecondary), maxHeight 220 + scrollable. Per the user's pick (inline list as you type, over a help-button/dialog). flutter analyze clean; 1307 tests pass; flutter build macos --debug green.

2026-06-22 (UTC) — Scene Guests: UNDO for an accidental /exit
Files changed: lib/services/chat/chat_command_handler.dart (new armExitUndo callback, called after the departure turn), lib/services/chat_service.dart (exit-undo state + armSceneGuestExitUndo/undoLastExit/_clearExitUndo + getters + wiring + invalidation on real-message/reset), lib/ui/pages/chat_page.dart (UNDO SnackBar), test/services/chat/chat_command_handler_test.dart (+2), docs/Rawhide.md, .claude/changelog.md.
Brief reason: User wanted to undo an accidental /exit — delete the generated departure message AND restore the guest with full context. Implemented as a brief UNDO SnackBar after /exit. Mechanics: the handler calls armExitUndo(target) AFTER the departure turn generates; ChatService.armSceneGuestExitUndo captures the just-generated host message (the departure) + the guest + sets a one-shot offer name (notify). chat_page observes exitUndoOfferName, consumes it (shows once), and shows a SnackBar "<name> left the scene" with an UNDO action (8s). undoLastExit() deletes the captured departure message via the EXISTING deleteMessage(index) — which already does the realism time-travel rollback (restores bond/trust/emotion/needs from the prior message's realism_state snapshot), so the host realism the goodbye applied is reverted, not just hidden — then re-adds the guest's id (their _guestEvolutionCounts/_evolvedPersonalities + RAG memory were never wiped by /exit, so re-adding restores full context) and re-resolves + saves. The undo is invalidated when the user sends a real message (_clearExitUndo before adding the user message) and at every scene-guest reset site (folded into _resetGuestActivityState). REUSE: leans on deleteMessage's existing rollback (no parallel revert path) and the fact that /exit is non-destructive to guest state. flutter analyze clean; 1308 tests pass (2 new: /exit arms undo for the exited guest; a failed /exit does not arm undo); flutter build macos --debug green.
2026-06-21 (UTC) — JSON card export: unify export envelope + add repository import test (follow-ups to PR #60)
Files changed: lib/services/v2_card_service.dart, test/services/character_repository_test.dart, docs/Rawhide.md (merge-resolved), .claude/changelog.md (this entry).
Brief reason: Merged MisterLotto's PR #60 (export cards as .json + fix raw .json import) into a Rawhide-targeted branch and addressed two review findings. (1) Interop asymmetry: the new saveCardAsJson wrote a proper Character Card V2 envelope ({spec: chara_card_v2, spec_version, data}), but PNG export (saveCardAsPng / encodeCharacterCardToPngBytes) still embedded the legacy flat data map with no spec marker — so a Front Porch PNG handed to SillyTavern/Risu lacked the standard V2 marker the JSON export now had. Introduced one shared private helper _buildCardV2Envelope(card) and routed all three export paths through it, so every exported card (PNG chunk + standalone .json) carries the same canonical envelope. Safe because readCard/parseCardJson already accept both the envelope ('data') and legacy flat shapes, and every chara-decoding test uses charaJson['data'] ?? charaJson. (2) Test gap: the user-facing fix (importing a raw .json must route through readCardFromJsonFile and synthesize a placeholder avatar instead of producing an empty name-only card) had no repository-level coverage — only V2CardService parse tests. Added a CharacterRepository DB-integration test that writes a standalone .json via saveCardAsJson, imports it through repo.importCharacter, and asserts fields + lorebook survive, a placeholder .png is synthesized and exists on disk, and the character lands in the in-memory list. Verification: no local Flutter/Dart SDK in this environment, so analyze/test are gated on CI via the PR into Rawhide (per maintainer decision) rather than run locally.

## 2026-06-22 — Unify chat UI (phase 1–2 of one-UI refactor): cast model + single message resolver + single AppBar
- Files: NEW lib/models/chat_participant.dart; lib/models/models.dart (export); lib/services/chat_service.dart (`cast` getter + import); lib/ui/pages/chat_page.dart (`_resolveSpeaker`, unified `_buildAppBar`, removed `_buildGroupAppBar` + duplicated sender-resolution branch)
- Reason: First steps toward a single chat UI for 1:1, Scene-Guest (Lite NPC), and group chats (SillyTavern model: a single chat is a cast of one, a group is the same chat with more participants), per the approved plan. PR #65 (Scene Guests) had already made the 1:1 page multi-speaker, leaving two near-identical message speaker-resolution branches and two parallel AppBars. Introduced `ChatParticipant` (thin read-only view over CharacterCard; `isHost`/`realismEnabled`/`isLite` derived from the card) and `ChatService.cast` (host+guests for 1:1/NPC, members for group). `_resolveSpeaker` replaces both old message branches with one path (coloring preserved exactly: non-host speakers colored by order among non-host participants, host uncolored, departed sender → placeholder). `_buildAppBar(context, chatService)` replaces both headers: cast of one = single avatar header, cast of 2+ = stacked avatars + "N characters" subtitle (group keeps name + turnOrder; emotion rings/tooltips unchanged when group realism active).
- Verification: established a green baseline (`flutter analyze` "No issues found!" on pristine Rawhide), then `flutter analyze --no-fatal-warnings --no-fatal-infos` clean after each change. Flutter 3.41.1 SDK installed in-session. Golden regeneration deferred to a follow-up after manual smoke (per plan).

## 2026-06-23 — chat_service.dart god-file thinning (part-file extractions)
- New part files under lib/services/chat/: chat_service_group_read.dart, chat_service_group_settings.dart, chat_service_evolution.dart, chat_service_sillytavern.dart, chat_service_group_realism_helpers.dart, chat_service_history.dart. Each is `part of '../chat_service.dart'` with an `extension ... on ChatService`.
- Reason: User asked to leave the realism/needs ENGINE as-is but aggressively thin the god file. Moved cohesive method clusters verbatim (zero behaviour change): group per-character realism read accessors; group RAG/memory + per-char author-note/system-prompt settings; character-evolution accessors + manual edit/reset/load; SillyTavern import/export; low-level group-realism map helpers (_getGroupNeeds etc.); chat-history builders + token counting.
- Pitfalls handled: (1) extension members are statically dispatched, so members overridden by `FakeChatService implements ChatService` must stay in-class — kept `characterEvolutionCount` as an instance getter for that reason. (2) Extensions can't declare instance fields — all backing fields stayed in the main library. (3) Static members must be qualified inside extensions — `_macroPattern` → `ChatService._macroPattern`.
- Result: chat_service.dart 10,506 → 9,852 lines (-654). flutter analyze clean (0 warnings); unit suite 1334 + golden suite together 1428 all green.
- Commits: 7b27f39, c1b5af3, 3f42608, 44c19f8.
